Biography

A Decade of Innovation
& Global Reach

As the Founder and Technical Lead of 'Min Kavi', I have spent the last 10 years building a comprehensive ecosystem that merges publishing, software development, and international supply chain logistics. Operating a global network that exports to over 10 countries, I specialize in transforming raw ideas into world-class digital and physical assets. My work is defined by precision, scale, and an unwavering commitment to quality.

Recognition

Prestige & Recognition

I
i
Heads of State & Icons of Industry

Works designed and published under my leadership have reached the hands of the Honorable Prime Minister of India, the Chief Minister of Tamil Nadu, and Infosys Chairperson Sudha Murty — a testament to the cultural resonance and calibre of our publications.

II
ii
In the Library of Legends

Books authored by me proudly hold a place in the personal library of Oscar-winning composer A.R. Rahman — a distinction reserved for works of exceptional literary and artistic merit.

Achievements

Personal Creative Achievements

4×
World Records

An Officially Recognised World Record Holder

An accomplished author and poet, I officially hold 4 World Records for pioneering literary achievements — specifically for the extraordinary fusion of technology with classical poetic forms. My signature genre, Tech Haiku, stands as a globally recognised innovation at the intersection of ancient verse and modern computation. Each record is a milestone in a body of work that refuses to separate art from engineering.

Author · Poet

Distinguished Published Portfolio

A distinguished portfolio of self-authored books available globally, including the renowned Tech Haiku collection — a body of work that has captivated audiences across borders and earned international critical acclaim for its unique synthesis of precision and lyricism.

Innovation · Literary Arts

Technology Meets Timeless Verse

By encoding the language of artificial intelligence, software architecture, and digital systems into the strict syllabic structure of Haiku, I created an entirely new literary genre — one that has redefined what it means to be both a technologist and a poet in the modern era.

Engineering

Driving the Future of Tech

01
Python · Streamlit · AI

Proprietary Publishing & Linguistic Software

Developed Valluvar 2.0 and Otru — proprietary tools engineered entirely with Python and Streamlit — seamlessly integrating artificial intelligence into traditional Tamil literary frameworks, redefining how ancient culture interfaces with modern computation.

02
Web Architecture · ISRO

Scientific Web Leadership

Served as Technical Lead and Web Developer for Valarum Ariviyal e-magazine — a platform closely associated with ISRO Scientist and Chandrayaan Project Director, Dr. Mayilsamy Annadurai. Also architected their fully integrated donation platform and digital infrastructure.

Global Reach

Purpose-Driven Expansion

"Scale without soul is just noise. Every project I build carries a purpose greater than profit."

Social Empowerment

68 Seniors. 68 Stories. One Movement.

Successfully guided and transitioned 68 senior citizens into published e-book authors, providing a digital platform to share their life experiences — a transformative initiative that eradicated the isolation of their golden years and gave timeless wisdom its rightful global audience.

International Projects

Digital Bridges Across Borders

Architected digital portals for the Brampton Tamil Seniors Association (Canada) and designed pandemic-era special publications for the Canadian Government — bringing Tamil voices to global platforms with precision and cultural authenticity.

Business Expansion

The Next Frontier

Currently expanding operations into Sea Cargo Logistics, academic ISSN Journal publishing, and integrating eco-friendly textile packaging — the traditional Manjappai — into the global supply chain. Heritage and innovation, unified.

Let's Connect

Open to strategic collaborations
and visionary projects.
